[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- During dissection, the function `dissect_bat_vis_v24` invokes a `printf`-style [0m   [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mformat tokens in the input, this also suggests a format-string–related issue, [0m      [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Root Cause Analysis[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The crash arises because `d_output_buffer`, which is built via `snprintf` [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39musing the untrusted `vis_packeth_raw_data` as a `%s` argument, is then passed [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdirectly to `[0m[1;35mfprintf[0m[1;39m([0m[39mstderr, d_output_buffer[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`. This treats the buffer contents as [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39ma format string, so any `%` sequences in packet data [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., `%x`, `%n`, `%s`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m will [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbe interpreted by `fprintf` and cause invalid reads.[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Additionally, the raw-data buffer `vis_packeth_raw_data` is filled [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbyte‐by‐byte without appending a terminating NUL character, so calls to `[0m[1;35mstrlen[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mor `%s` formatting on it may read beyond its valid contents.[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Preservation of Critical Logic[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - We must preserve:[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • The condition that only logs raw-data when `vis_packeth_raw_data_size > [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m` [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand the string length exceeds [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m.[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • The content of `d_output_buffer`, which provides human-readable diagnostics [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfor the dissector.[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - We must continue using the same fuzzing API and harness logic [0m[1;39m([0m[39mno changes to [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfuzz harness[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Patch Steps[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   A. Null-Terminate the Raw-Data Buffer[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      • Immediately after the loop copying `vis_packeth_raw_data_size` bytes, [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mappend a NUL character. This ensures safe use in `snprintf` and `strlen`.[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      • If `vis_packeth_raw_data_size` equals the maximum buffer length, explicitly[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mNUL-terminate the last slot.[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      Pseudocode insertion [0m[1;39m([0m[39mafter line [0m[1;36m671[0m[39m in packet-bat.c[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        vis_packeth_raw_data[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mvis_packeth_raw_data_size < [0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35msizeof[0m[1;39m([0m[39mvis_packeth_raw_data[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                             ? vis_packeth_raw_data_size[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                             : [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35msizeof[0m[1;39m([0m[39mvis_packeth_raw_data[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m - [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = [0m[32m'\0'[0m[39m;[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   B. Safely Print the Formatted Buffer[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      • Replace the unsafe `[0m[1;35mfprintf[0m[1;39m([0m[39mstderr, d_output_buffer[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;` call with a safe [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvariant that treats `d_output_buffer` as data, not a format:[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        – Option [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m: `[0m[1;35mfprintf[0m[1;39m([0m[39mstderr, [0m[32m"%s"[0m[39m, d_output_buffer[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        – Option [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m: `[0m[1;35mfputs[0m[1;39m([0m[39md_output_buffer, stderr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      • Either approach prevents interpretation of `%` tokens in the buffer.[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      Pseudocode replacement [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m704[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m705[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mvis_packeth_raw_data_size > [0m[1;36m4[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m && [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mstrlen[0m[1;39m([0m[39mvis_packeth_raw_data[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m > [0m[1;36m4[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m{[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            [0m[35m/[0m[39m* Safe print of raw-data diagnostics *[0m[35m/[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            [0m[1;35mfprintf[0m[1;39m([0m[39mstderr, [0m[32m"%s"[0m[39m, d_output_buffer[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Justification[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Null-terminating `vis_packeth_raw_data` ensures all subsequent string [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moperations [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`strlen`, `%s` in `snprintf`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m only read valid, in-bounds data.[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Changing `fprintf` to use an explicit format string eliminates the [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mformat-string vulnerability, preventing `%` sequences from causing unintended reads[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mor writes.[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - These changes are localized to `dissect_bat_vis_v24` and do not alter external[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlibraries, harness code, or tests.[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The existing logic for when to log diagnostics remains exactly the same, so no[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexisting functionality is broken.[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Potential Side Effects and Mitigation[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - There is a negligible performance impact from the extra NUL assignment.[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Logging output remains identical, except that stray `%` characters will now [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mappear verbatim rather than triggering formatting errors.[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No other parts of the codebase rely on non-terminated `vis_packeth_raw_data`; [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mif they did, they will now behave more safely.[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Similar Patterns in Codebase[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Other dissectors often null-terminate raw buffers before formatting, e.g., in [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`packet-xyz.c` they use:[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       raw_data[0m[1;39m[[0m[39msize < RAW_MAX ? size : RAW_MAX-[0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = [0m[32m'\0'[0m[39m;[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - They also consistently use `[0m[1;35mfprintf[0m[1;39m([0m[39mstderr, [0m[32m"%s"[0m[39m, msg[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` for diagnostic [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmessages.[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code_range>epan/dissectors/packet-bat.[0m[1;92mc:668[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m672[0m[39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_range[0m[39m>[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code_range>epan/dissectors/packet-bat.[0m[1;92mc:704[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m705[0m[39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_range[0m[39m>[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
